    44	import {
    45	  readStoredObjectMap,
    46	  resolveProjectKey,
    47	  STORAGE_KEY_PREFIX,
    48	} from './swimlane-storage.ts';
    49	
    50	const LANE_COLLAPSE_KEY_SUFFIX = ':lane-collapse';
    51	const STAGE_COLLAPSE_KEY_SUFFIX = ':stage-collapse';
    52	
    53	interface CollapseState {
    54	  /** Lane ids the operator has lane-collapsed. */
    55	  readonly lanes: Set<string>;
    56	  /** Lane id → set of collapsed stage names within that lane. */
    57	  readonly stages: Map<string, Set<string>>;
    58	}
    59	
    60	function laneCollapseKey(projectKey: string): string {
    61	  return STORAGE_KEY_PREFIX + projectKey + LANE_COLLAPSE_KEY_SUFFIX;
    62	}
    63	
    64	function stageCollapseKey(projectKey: string): string {
    65	  return STORAGE_KEY_PREFIX + projectKey + STAGE_COLLAPSE_KEY_SUFFIX;
    66	}
    67	
    68	function readStoredLanes(key: string): Set<string> {
    69	  try {
    70	    const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(key);
    71	    if (raw === null) return new Set<string>();
    72	    const parsed: unknown = JSON.parse(raw);
    73	    if (!Array.isArray(parsed)) return new Set<string>();
    74	    const out = new Set<string>();
    75	    for (const item of parsed) {
    76	      if (typeof item === 'string') out.add(item);
    77	    }
    78	    return out;
    79	  } catch {
    80	    return new Set<string>();
    81	  }
    82	}
    83	
    84	function isStringArray(value: unknown): value is readonly string[] {
    85	  return Array.isArray(value) && value.every((v) => typeof v === 'string');
    86	}
    87	
    88	function readStoredStages(key: string): Map<string, Set<string>> {
    89	  // The on-disk shape is `Record<laneId, string[]>` — sets are
    90	  // serialised as arrays. Use the shared object-map reader to get
    91	  // a `Map<laneId, string[]>`, then post-process into the in-memory
    92	  // `Map<laneId, Set<string>>`, dropping empty sets.
    93	  const arrays = readStoredObjectMap<readonly string[]>(key, isStringArray);
    94	  const out = new Map<string, Set<string>>();
    95	  for (const [laneId, items] of arrays) {
    96	    const stages = new Set<string>(items);
    97	    if (stages.size > 0) out.set(laneId, stages);
    98	  }
    99	  return out;
   100	}
   101	
   102	function writeStoredLanes(key: string, value: ReadonlySet<string>): void {
   103	  try {
   104	    window.localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(Array.from(value)));
   105	  } catch {
   106	    // localStorage unavailable — in-page state still works.
   107	  }
   108	}
   109	
   110	function writeStoredStages(
   111	  key: string,
   112	  value: ReadonlyMap<string, ReadonlySet<string>>,
   113	): void {
   114	  try {
   115	    const out: Record<string, string[]> = {};
   116	    for (const [laneId, stages] of value) {
   117	      if (stages.size === 0) continue;
   118	      out[laneId] = Array.from(stages);
   119	    }
   120	    window.localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(out));
   121	  } catch {
   122	    // localStorage unavailable — in-page state still works.
   123	  }
   124	}
   125	
   126	/**
   127	 * Apply current collapse state to the DOM: toggle `.collapsed` on
   128	 * targets, set `aria-expanded` on the matching chevrons.
   129	 */
   130	function applyCollapseState(state: CollapseState): void {
   131	  // Lane-level collapse: `.swim[data-lane-id]`.
   132	  for (const swim of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>('.swim[data-lane-id]')) {
   133	    const laneId = swim.dataset.laneId;
   134	    if (laneId === undefined) continue;
   135	    const collapsed = state.lanes.has(laneId);
   136	    swim.classList.toggle('collapsed', collapsed);
   137	    const chev = swim.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>(
   138	      '.swim-head > .collapse-chev[data-collapse-target="lane"]',
   139	    );
   140	    if (chev !== null) {
   141	      chev.setAttribute('aria-expanded', collapsed ? 'false' : 'true');
   142	      const humanName = chev.dataset.laneName ?? laneId;
   143	      chev.setAttribute(
   144	        'aria-label',
   145	        `${collapsed ? 'Expand' : 'Collapse'} ${humanName} lane`,
   146	      );
   147	    }
   148	  }
   149	
   150	  // Per-stage collapse — kanban scope (`.stage-col[data-stage-col]`)
   151	  // + list-body scope (`.lb-group[data-lb-group]`). Both views share
   152	  // the same lane:stage state — a stage collapsed in one view shows
   153	  // collapsed in the other (the operator's mental model of "this
   154	  // stage is folded" is view-independent).
   155	  applyStageScope(state, {
   156	    parentSelector: '.stage-col[data-stage-col]',
   157	    stageAttrKey: 'stageCol',
   158	    chevSelector: '.stage-head > .collapse-chev[data-collapse-target="stage"]',
   159	    labelNoun: 'stage',
   160	  });
   161	  applyStageScope(state, {
   162	    parentSelector: '.lb-group[data-lb-group]',
   163	    stageAttrKey: 'lbGroup',
   164	    chevSelector: '.lb-group-head > .collapse-chev[data-collapse-target="stage"]',
   165	    labelNoun: 'group',
   166	  });
   167	}
   168	
   169	interface StageScopeConfig {
   170	  /** CSS selector for the per-stage parent element. */
   171	  readonly parentSelector: string;
   172	  /** Dataset key on the parent that carries the stage name. */
   173	  readonly stageAttrKey: string;
   174	  /** CSS selector for the chevron button inside the parent. */
   175	  readonly chevSelector: string;
   176	  /** Noun appended to the aria-label (e.g. "stage" or "group"). */
   177	  readonly labelNoun: string;
   178	}
   179	
   180	function applyStageScope(state: CollapseState, cfg: StageScopeConfig): void {
   181	  for (const parent of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>(cfg.parentSelector)) {
   182	    const stageName = parent.dataset[cfg.stageAttrKey];
   183	    if (stageName === undefined) continue;
   184	    const swim = parent.closest<HTMLElement>('.swim[data-lane-id]');
   185	    const laneId = swim?.dataset.laneId;
   186	    if (laneId === undefined) continue;
   187	    const stages = state.stages.get(laneId);
   188	    const collapsed = stages !== undefined && stages.has(stageName);
   189	    parent.classList.toggle('collapsed', collapsed);
   190	    const chev = parent.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>(cfg.chevSelector);
   191	    if (chev !== null) {
   192	      chev.setAttribute('aria-expanded', collapsed ? 'false' : 'true');
   193	      chev.setAttribute(
   194	        'aria-label',
   195	        `${collapsed ? 'Expand' : 'Collapse'} ${stageName} ${cfg.labelNoun}`,
   196	      );
   197	    }
   198	  }
   199	}
   200	
   201	function persist(state: CollapseState, projectKey: string): void {
   202	  writeStoredLanes(laneCollapseKey(projectKey), state.lanes);
   203	  writeStoredStages(stageCollapseKey(projectKey), state.stages);
   204	}
   205	
   206	function toggleLane(state: CollapseState, laneId: string): void {
   207	  if (state.lanes.has(laneId)) {
   208	    state.lanes.delete(laneId);
   209	  } else {
   210	    state.lanes.add(laneId);
   211	  }
   212	}
   213	
   214	function toggleStage(
   215	  state: CollapseState,
   216	  laneId: string,
   217	  stageName: string,
   218	): void {
   219	  let stages = state.stages.get(laneId);
   220	  if (stages === undefined) {
   221	    stages = new Set<string>();
   222	    state.stages.set(laneId, stages);
   223	  }
   224	  if (stages.has(stageName)) {
   225	    stages.delete(stageName);
   226	    if (stages.size === 0) state.stages.delete(laneId);
   227	  } else {
   228	    stages.add(stageName);
   229	  }
   230	}
   231	
   232	/**
   233	 * Resolve a click/keyboard activation on a chevron OR on its
   234	 * enclosing head into a lane-or-stage toggle. Returns true when a
   235	 * toggle fired so the caller can persist + reapply.
   236	 */
   237	function dispatchToggle(
   238	  state: CollapseState,
   239	  target: HTMLElement,
   240	): boolean {
   241	  // Prefer the chevron's data attributes when the click landed on
   242	  // (or inside) one — that's the authoritative source.
   243	  const chev = target.closest<HTMLElement>('.collapse-chev');
   244	  if (chev !== null) {
   245	    const scope = chev.dataset.collapseTarget;
   246	    const laneId = chev.dataset.laneId;
   247	    if (laneId === undefined) return false;
   248	    if (scope === 'lane') {
   249	      toggleLane(state, laneId);
   250	      return true;
   251	    }
   252	    if (scope === 'stage') {
   253	      const stageName = chev.dataset.stageName;
   254	      if (stageName === undefined) return false;
   255	      toggleStage(state, laneId, stageName);
   256	      return true;
   257	    }
   258	    return false;
   259	  }
   260	
   261	  // Fall back to the head element — clicking anywhere on the head
   262	  // (per the affordance contract) toggles the affordance.
   263	  const stageHead = target.closest<HTMLElement>('.stage-head');
   264	  if (stageHead !== null) {
   265	    const col = stageHead.closest<HTMLElement>('.stage-col[data-stage-col]');
   266	    const stageName = col?.dataset.stageCol;
   267	    const swim = col?.closest<HTMLElement>('.swim[data-lane-id]');
   268	    const laneId = swim?.dataset.laneId;
   269	    if (laneId === undefined || stageName === undefined) return false;
   270	    toggleStage(state, laneId, stageName);
   271	    return true;
   272	  }
   273	
   274	  // List-body group head — same per-stage contract, different
   275	  // parent element. Per Task 5.1B the lane:stage state is shared
   276	  // with kanban so the toggle applies across both views.
   277	  const groupHead = target.closest<HTMLElement>('.lb-group-head');
   278	  if (groupHead !== null) {
   279	    const group = groupHead.closest<HTMLElement>('.lb-group[data-lb-group]');
   280	    const stageName = group?.dataset.lbGroup;
   281	    const swim = group?.closest<HTMLElement>('.swim[data-lane-id]');
   282	    const laneId = swim?.dataset.laneId;
   283	    if (laneId === undefined || stageName === undefined) return false;
   284	    toggleStage(state, laneId, stageName);
   285	    return true;
   286	  }
   287	
   288	  const swimHead = target.closest<HTMLElement>('.swim-head');
   289	  if (swimHead !== null) {
   290	    const swim = swimHead.closest<HTMLElement>('.swim[data-lane-id]');
   291	    const laneId = swim?.dataset.laneId;
   292	    if (laneId === undefined) return false;
   293	    toggleLane(state, laneId);
   294	    return true;
   295	  }
   296	
   297	  return false;
   298	}
   299	
   300	/**
   301	 * Stage-level dispatch: when the click is inside the stage-head OR
   302	 * the column is currently collapsed (so any click on the narrow
   303	 * strip should re-expand), fire the stage toggle. Otherwise the
   304	 * click is on a card inside an expanded column — defer to the
   305	 * card's own handler.
   306	 */
   307	function dispatchToggleStage(
   308	  state: CollapseState,
   309	  target: HTMLElement,
   310	  col: HTMLElement,
   311	): boolean {
   312	  const stageName = col.dataset.stageCol;
   313	  const swim = col.closest<HTMLElement>('.swim[data-lane-id]');
   314	  const laneId = swim?.dataset.laneId;
   315	  if (laneId === undefined || stageName === undefined) return false;
   316	
   317	  const inHead = target.closest<HTMLElement>('.stage-head') !== null;
   318	  const isCollapsed = col.classList.contains('collapsed');
   319	  if (!inHead && !isCollapsed) return false;
   320	
   321	  toggleStage(state, laneId, stageName);
   322	  return true;
   323	}
   324	
   325	/**
   326	 * List-body group dispatch: mirror of `dispatchToggleStage` but
   327	 * scoped to `.lb-group` containers. The list-body lb-row carries
   328	 * its own `<a>` semantics (open the entry-review surface), so the
   329	 * group toggle fires only when the click lands on the group head
   330	 * — clicking a row navigates instead of collapsing the group.
   331	 */
   332	function dispatchToggleListGroup(
   333	  state: CollapseState,
   334	  target: HTMLElement,
   335	  group: HTMLElement,
   336	): boolean {
   337	  const stageName = group.dataset.lbGroup;
   338	  const swim = group.closest<HTMLElement>('.swim[data-lane-id]');
   339	  const laneId = swim?.dataset.laneId;
   340	  if (laneId === undefined || stageName === undefined) return false;
   341	
   342	  const inHead = target.closest<HTMLElement>('.lb-group-head') !== null;
   343	  if (!inHead) return false;
   344	
   345	  toggleStage(state, laneId, stageName);
   346	  return true;
   347	}
   348	
   349	function bindHandlers(state: CollapseState, projectKey: string): void {
   350	  // Lane-level: click on swim-head (anywhere) toggles. The chevron is
   351	  // a child of the swim-head so its click bubbles through this handler.
   352	  // The 5.1B view-toggle + 5.1C compose chip will live inside the
   353	  // same swim-head; once they ship their own click handlers will need
   354	  // to `event.stopPropagation()` so the lane-collapse handler doesn't
   355	  // fire on their gestures.
   356	  for (const head of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>('.swim-head')) {
   357	    head.addEventListener('click', (ev) => {
   358	      const target = ev.target;
   359	      if (!(target instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
   360	      if (!dispatchToggle(state, target)) return;
   361	      applyCollapseState(state);
   362	      persist(state, projectKey);
   363	    });
   364	  }
   365	
   366	  // Per-stage: click anywhere on the stage-col toggles. The stage-
   367	  // head + chevron are children of stage-col so their clicks bubble
   368	  // through. When the column is collapsed (narrow vertical strip,
   369	  // mockup line 612 `.stage-col.collapsed { cursor: pointer }`)
   370	  // clicking anywhere on the strip re-expands it; `dispatchToggle`'s
   371	  // fallback covers that via `target.closest('.stage-head')`.
   372	  // Cards inside an expanded column carry their own click handlers
   373	  // and use stopPropagation; the toggle fires only on stage-head
   374	  // gestures and on the collapsed-strip background.
   375	  for (const col of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>('.stage-col')) {
   376	    col.addEventListener('click', (ev) => {
   377	      const target = ev.target;
   378	      if (!(target instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
   379	      if (!dispatchToggleStage(state, target, col)) return;
   380	      applyCollapseState(state);
   381	      persist(state, projectKey);
   382	    });
   383	  }
   384	
   385	  // Per-stage (list-body scope): click on the `.lb-group-head`
   386	  // toggles. The list-body has `.lb-row` anchor links inside the
   387	  // group; clicking a row navigates via its own `<a>` semantics —
   388	  // `dispatchToggleListGroup` only fires when the target is inside
   389	  // the head so a row click doesn't accidentally collapse its
   390	  // group on the way to the entry-review surface.
   391	  for (const group of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>('.lb-group[data-lb-group]')) {
   392	    group.addEventListener('click', (ev) => {
   393	      const target = ev.target;
   394	      if (!(target instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
   395	      if (!dispatchToggleListGroup(state, target, group)) return;
   396	      applyCollapseState(state);
   397	      persist(state, projectKey);
   398	    });
   399	  }
   400	
   401	  // Keyboard: Enter + Space on the chevron buttons activate the
   402	  // toggle. The `<button>` element gets click-on-Enter for free; we
   403	  // bind Space explicitly so we can preventDefault the page scroll
   404	  // (per WCAG 2.1 SC 2.1.1 keyboard accessibility — the focusable
   405	  // button must not trigger an unrelated default action).
   406	  for (const chev of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>('.collapse-chev')) {
   407	    chev.addEventListener('keydown', (ev) => {
   408	      if (ev.key !== ' ') return;
   409	      ev.preventDefault();
   410	      if (!dispatchToggle(state, chev)) return;
   411	      applyCollapseState(state);
   412	      persist(state, projectKey);
   413	    });
   414	  }
   415	}
   416	
   417	/**
   418	 * Module-level singleton — written by `initSwimlaneCollapse`,
   419	 * mutated in-place by `reapplyCollapseFromStorage` so the bound
   420	 * `swim-head` / `stage-col` click handlers (which closure-capture
   421	 * the state object) keep operating on the same Sets / Maps after a
   422	 * preset apply. See `swimlane.ts:activeState` for the same pattern
   423	 * + rationale.
   424	 *
   425	 * Per AUDIT-20260528-37 (F5): tests that mutate this singleton must
   426	 * reset DOM + storage in `beforeEach` so cross-describe-block state
   427	 * does not leak. There is no `resetActiveState()` export — the
   428	 * singleton's lifecycle is bound to `initSwimlaneCollapse`, which
   429	 * reassigns it. Rebuilding the page shell + re-invoking init is the
   430	 * sanctioned reset path.
   431	 */
   432	let activeState: CollapseState | null = null;
   433	
   434	/**
   435	 * Re-read storage + re-apply to the DOM. Used by the Task 5.5
   436	 * preset controller after writing through the lane-collapse + stage-
   437	 * collapse storage keys. No-op when `initSwimlaneCollapse` hasn't
   438	 * fired yet (controllers run in order at DOMContentLoaded).
   439	 */
   440	export function reapplyCollapseFromStorage(): void {
   441	  if (activeState === null) return;
   442	  const shell = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>('[data-bay-shell]');
   443	  if (shell === null) return;
   444	  const projectKey = resolveProjectKey(shell);
   445	
   446	  const nextLanes = readStoredLanes(laneCollapseKey(projectKey));
   447	  const nextStages = readStoredStages(stageCollapseKey(projectKey));
   448	
   449	  // Mutate the singleton in-place so already-bound handlers see the
   450	  // new lane + stage state through their closure-captured references.
   451	  activeState.lanes.clear();
   452	  for (const id of nextLanes) activeState.lanes.add(id);
   453	  activeState.stages.clear();
   454	  for (const [laneId, stages] of nextStages) {
   455	    activeState.stages.set(laneId, stages);
   456	  }
   457	  applyCollapseState(activeState);
   458	}
   459	
   460	/**

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	/**
     2	 * Multi-lane swimlane dashboard controller (Phase 5 Task 5.1).
     3	 *
     4	 * Wires the bay shell's focus-chip strip + lane-visibility rail to
     5	 * persistent per-operator state stored in localStorage. The server
     6	 * renders the initial paint from a `?focus=<csv>` URL param (or "all
     7	 * focused" when absent); the client controller takes over once
     8	 * `DOMContentLoaded` fires and:
     9	 *
    10	 *   - Reads `?focus=` from `window.location.search`. If present, the
    11	 *     URL wins on this load AND is written through to localStorage so
    12	 *     subsequent loads (without the param) see the URL-set focus.
    13	 *   - Otherwise reads the focus set from localStorage and applies it.
    14	 *   - Reads the visibility set from localStorage and hides any lane
    15	 *     the operator has flipped persistently OFF (eye-toggle in the
    16	 *     rail).
    17	 *
    18	 * Click handlers:
    19	 *
    20	 *   - Focus chip: toggles whether the lane is in the focus set.
    21	 *     "All" chip resets focus to every visible lane.
    22	 *   - Rail eye-toggle (clicking the `.r-eye-btn` button — F6 a11y
    23	 *     fix promoted the previous `.r-eye` span to a real focusable
    24	 *     `<button>`): flips persistent visibility.
    25	 *   - Rail row keyboard activation (F5 a11y fix): Enter / Space on
    26	 *     a `.rail-lane[role="button"]` toggles focus state (mirrors the
    27	 *     click handler bound on the same element).
    28	 *   - Swim-stub: re-adds the lane to focus (the stub removes itself
    29	 *     once the swimlane renders).
    30	 *
    31	 * State keys are namespaced per project root so two operators
    32	 * sharing a machine but working on different projects don't see
    33	 * each other's focus state. The project-root hash is server-rendered
    34	 * onto `<section class="bay-shell" data-project-key>`.
    35	 *
    36	 * Out of scope for 5.1: lane-level collapse (5.1A), per-stage
    37	 * collapse (5.1A), kanban ↔ list toggle (5.1B), compose chip (5.1C),
    38	 * drag reorder (5.4), preset save (5.5).
    39	 */
    40	
    41	import {
    42	  readStoredStringArray,
    43	  resolveProjectKey,
    44	  STORAGE_KEY_PREFIX,
    45	} from './swimlane-storage.ts';
    46	
    47	const FOCUS_KEY_SUFFIX = ':focus';
    48	const VISIBILITY_KEY_SUFFIX = ':visibility';
    49	
    50	interface SwimlaneState {
    51	  /** Set of lane ids currently focused. */
    52	  readonly focused: Set<string>;
    53	  /**
    54	   * Set of lane ids the operator has flipped persistently OFF in
    55	   * the rail. Visibility-off lanes are removed from the focus-chip
    56	   * strip and don't render in the bay; the operator must flip them
    57	   * back ON via the rail to see them again.
    58	   */
    59	  readonly hidden: Set<string>;
    60	  /** All lane ids known to the page (server-rendered ordering). */
    61	  readonly allLanes: readonly string[];
    62	}
    63	
    64	function focusKey(projectKey: string): string {
    65	  return STORAGE_KEY_PREFIX + projectKey + FOCUS_KEY_SUFFIX;
    66	}
    67	
    68	function visibilityKey(projectKey: string): string {
    69	  return STORAGE_KEY_PREFIX + projectKey + VISIBILITY_KEY_SUFFIX;
    70	}
    71	
    72	function readStoredSet(key: string): Set<string> | null {
    73	  // Delegates to the shared string-array reader in swimlane-storage.ts
    74	  // (the read+parse boilerplate); this surface returns a Set because
    75	  // the focus + hidden state is set-shaped (membership matters,
    76	  // order does not). The order surface in swimlane-drag.ts uses the
    77	  // same reader but keeps the positional array.
    78	  const items = readStoredStringArray(key);
    79	  if (items === null) return null;
    80	  return new Set(items);
    81	}
    82	
    83	function writeStoredSet(key: string, value: ReadonlySet<string>): void {
    84	  try {
    85	    window.localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(Array.from(value)));
    86	  } catch {
    87	    // localStorage unavailable — the client controller still works
    88	    // in-page; the operator just loses persistence across reloads.
    89	  }
    90	}
    91	
    92	function parseFocusFromUrl(): Set<string> | null {
    93	  const url = new URL(window.location.href);
    94	  const list = parseCsvNonEmpty(url.searchParams.get('focus'));
    95	  return list === null ? null : new Set(list);
    96	}
    97	
    98	/**
    99	 * Parse a CSV string into a deduped non-empty list of trimmed items.
   100	 * Returns null when the input is null OR empty after trimming. Shared
   101	 * by `parseFocusFromUrl` here and (logically) by the server-side
   102	 * `parseFocusCsv` in the dashboard render path — both implement the
   103	 * same parsing contract on the same wire format. The shapes are
   104	 * deliberately near-identical; the duplication is a wire-format
   105	 * symmetry, not a refactor opportunity (server bundle and client
   106	 * bundle are separate; cross-bundle imports would force a shared
   107	 * vendored module).
   108	 */
   109	function parseCsvNonEmpty(raw: string | null): string[] | null {
   110	  if (raw === null) return null;
   111	  const parts = raw
   112	    .split(',')
   113	    .map((p) => p.trim())
   114	    .filter((p) => p.length > 0);
   115	  if (parts.length === 0) return null;
   116	  return parts;
   117	}
   118	
   119	function collectAllLanes(): string[] {
   120	  const ids: string[] = [];
   121	  for (const el of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>('[data-rail-lane]')) {
   122	    const id = el.dataset.railLane;
   123	    if (id !== undefined) ids.push(id);
   124	  }
   125	  return ids;
   126	}
   127	
   128	/**
   129	 * Apply the current state to the DOM: toggle `.is-focus-hidden` on
   130	 * swimlanes / swim-stubs, set chip `.active` state, set rail
   131	 * `aria-pressed` + `.focused` state, hide visibility-off lanes
   132	 * entirely.
   133	 */
   134	function applyState(state: SwimlaneState): void {
   135	  // Swimlanes and stubs.
   136	  for (const id of state.allLanes) {
   137	    const swim = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
   138	      `.swim[data-lane-id="${CSS.escape(id)}"]`,
   139	    );
   140	    const stub = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
   141	      `.swim-stub[data-swim-stub="${CSS.escape(id)}"]`,
   142	    );
   143	    const hidden = state.hidden.has(id);
   144	    const focused = state.focused.has(id);
   145	
   146	    if (swim !== null) {
   147	      swim.classList.toggle('is-visibility-hidden', hidden);
   148	      swim.classList.toggle('is-focus-hidden', !hidden && !focused);
   149	    }
   150	    if (stub !== null) {
   151	      stub.classList.toggle('is-visibility-hidden', hidden);
   152	      stub.classList.toggle('is-focus-hidden', hidden || focused);
   153	    }
   154	  }
   155	
   156	  // Focus chips.
   157	  for (const chip of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>(
   158	    '[data-focus-chip]',
   159	  )) {
   160	    const id = chip.dataset.focusChip;
   161	    if (id === undefined) continue;
   162	    const hidden = state.hidden.has(id);
   163	    const focused = state.focused.has(id);
   164	    chip.classList.toggle('active', focused && !hidden);
   165	    chip.classList.toggle('is-visibility-hidden', hidden);
   166	    chip.setAttribute('aria-pressed', focused && !hidden ? 'true' : 'false');
   167	  }
   168	
   169	  // "All" chip — active when every visible lane is focused.
   170	  const allChip = document.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>(
   171	    '[data-focus-chip-all]',
   172	  );
   173	  if (allChip !== null) {
   174	    const visibleLanes = state.allLanes.filter((id) => !state.hidden.has(id));
   175	    const allVisibleFocused =
   176	      visibleLanes.length > 0 &&
   177	      visibleLanes.every((id) => state.focused.has(id));
   178	    allChip.classList.toggle('active', allVisibleFocused);
   179	    allChip.setAttribute(
   180	      'aria-pressed',
   181	      allVisibleFocused ? 'true' : 'false',
   182	    );
   183	  }
   184	
   185	  // Rail rows.
   186	  for (const row of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>('[data-rail-lane]')) {
   187	    const id = row.dataset.railLane;
   188	    if (id === undefined) continue;
   189	    const hidden = state.hidden.has(id);
   190	    const focused = state.focused.has(id);
   191	    row.classList.toggle('focused', focused && !hidden);
   192	    row.dataset.laneVisible = hidden ? 'false' : 'true';
   193	    row.setAttribute('aria-pressed', focused && !hidden ? 'true' : 'false');
   194	  }
   195	}
   196	
   197	function persist(state: SwimlaneState, projectKey: string): void {
   198	  writeStoredSet(focusKey(projectKey), state.focused);
   199	  writeStoredSet(visibilityKey(projectKey), state.hidden);
   200	}
   201	
   202	/**
   203	 * Single shared focus toggle. Used by the per-lane focus chips —
   204	 * those callers never want to surface a hidden lane (the chip's CSS
   205	 * `is-visibility-hidden` rule hides it from the strip entirely).
   206	 * Returns true when the toggle actually fired (visible lanes); false
   207	 * when ignored (hidden lanes don't participate in focus from the
   208	 * chip path).
   209	 */
   210	function toggleFocus(
   211	  state: SwimlaneState,
   212	  projectKey: string,
   213	  id: string,
   214	): boolean {
   215	  if (state.hidden.has(id)) return false;
   216	  if (state.focused.has(id)) {
   217	    state.focused.delete(id);
   218	  } else {
   219	    state.focused.add(id);
   220	  }
   221	  applyState(state);
   222	  persist(state, projectKey);
   223	  return true;
   224	}
   225	
   226	/**
   227	 * Task 5.3.2 — rail-row activation contract: the rail acts as the
   228	 * master list of every lane (visible AND hidden). Clicking (or
   229	 * keyboard-activating) a rail row has a dual semantics:
   230	 *
   231	 *   - On a HIDDEN lane: flip visibility ON AND add the lane to focus
   232	 *     in a single gesture. This is the "bring it back" semantic the
   233	 *     rail exists to serve.
   234	 *   - On a VISIBLE lane: toggle focus on/off (the existing 5.1
   235	 *     behavior).
   236	 *
   237	 * The dedicated `.r-eye-btn` (handled separately) still exclusively
   238	 * toggles persistent visibility — its click path stays unchanged so
   239	 * the operator retains the "hide without focusing" gesture.
   240	 *
   241	 * Returns the activation kind so callers (e.g. the mobile-sheet
   242	 * controller) can chain additional behavior — closing the sheet on
   243	 * focus activation, for instance.
   244	 */
   245	type RailRowActivation = 'unhid-and-focused' | 'focus-toggled';
   246	
   247	export function handleRailRowActivation(
   248	  state: SwimlaneState,
   249	  projectKey: string,
   250	  id: string,
   251	): RailRowActivation {
   252	  if (state.hidden.has(id)) {
   253	    state.hidden.delete(id);
   254	    state.focused.add(id);
   255	    applyState(state);
   256	    persist(state, projectKey);
   257	    return 'unhid-and-focused';
   258	  }
   259	  toggleFocus(state, projectKey, id);
   260	  return 'focus-toggled';
   261	}
   262	
   263	function bindFocusChips(state: SwimlaneState, projectKey: string): void {
   264	  // Per-lane chips.
   265	  for (const chip of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>(
   266	    '[data-focus-chip]',
   267	  )) {
   268	    const id = chip.dataset.focusChip;
   269	    if (id === undefined) continue;
   270	    chip.addEventListener('click', () => {
   271	      toggleFocus(state, projectKey, id);
   272	    });
   273	  }
   274	
   275	  // "All" chip — focuses every visible lane. Idempotent: the spec
   276	  // ("focuses every visible lane") has no documented toggle-off
   277	  // semantics. The prior `isAlreadyAll`-gated branch left the focus
   278	  // set EMPTY when the operator clicked `All` while all lanes were
   279	  // already focused — silently un-focusing everything (AUDIT-20260528-09).
   280	  // The fix collapses to clear → add-all-visible regardless of prior
   281	  // state.
   282	  const allChip = document.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>(
   283	    '[data-focus-chip-all]',
   284	  );
   285	  if (allChip !== null) {
   286	    allChip.addEventListener('click', () => {
   287	      const allVisible = state.allLanes.filter((id) => !state.hidden.has(id));
   288	      state.focused.clear();
   289	      for (const id of allVisible) state.focused.add(id);
   290	      applyState(state);
   291	      persist(state, projectKey);
   292	    });
   293	  }
   294	}
   295	
   296	function bindRailEyeToggles(
   297	  state: SwimlaneState,
   298	  projectKey: string,
   299	): void {
   300	  // Clicking the rail row's eye glyph toggles persistent visibility;
   301	  // clicking elsewhere on the row toggles focus (default rail
   302	  // behavior). F5 a11y fix: the row carries `role="button"` so it
   303	  // must also honor Enter / Space activation via keyboard.
   304	  for (const row of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>(
   305	    '[data-rail-lane]',
   306	  )) {
   307	    const id = row.dataset.railLane;
   308	    if (id === undefined) continue;
   309	
   310	    // F6 a11y fix: the visibility toggle is a real `<button
   311	    // class="r-eye-btn">` (previously a span). Stops click
   312	    // propagation so the row's focus-toggle handler doesn't also
   313	    // fire on the same gesture.
   314	    const eye = row.querySelector<HTMLElement>('.r-eye-btn');
   315	    if (eye !== null) {
   316	      eye.addEventListener('click', (ev) => {
   317	        ev.stopPropagation();
   318	        if (state.hidden.has(id)) {
   319	          state.hidden.delete(id);
   320	        } else {
   321	          state.hidden.add(id);
   322	          state.focused.delete(id);
   323	        }
   324	        applyState(state);
   325	        persist(state, projectKey);
   326	      });
   327	    }
   328	
   329	    row.addEventListener('click', () => {
   330	      handleRailRowActivation(state, projectKey, id);
   331	    });
   332	
   333	    // F5 a11y fix: keyboard activation for the row's role="button".
   334	    // Enter and Space both activate; preventDefault on Space stops
   335	    // the default page-scroll. Per Task 5.3.2 the keyboard path
   336	    // mirrors the click path — both gestures dispatch through
   337	    // `handleRailRowActivation` so hidden-lane Enter unhides + focuses
   338	    // identically to click.
   339	    //
   340	    // Eye-button keyboard symmetry (AUDIT-20260528-06 / AUDIT-20260528-21):
   341	    // when an interactive descendant has keyboard focus, Enter/Space
   342	    // must trigger ITS OWN activation, not the row's dual-action handler.
   343	    // Without this guard the row's `preventDefault` cancels the native
   344	    // button activation and the descendant's contract is silently
   345	    // swallowed. The descendant's own click handler runs
   346	    // `stopPropagation` so the mouse path is already correct; this
   347	    // guard provides the symmetric keyboard path. We match any nested
   348	    // `button`, `a[href]`, `input`, `select`, `textarea`, or element
   349	    // carrying its own `role="button"` — not just `.r-eye-btn` — so
   350	    // future interactive children (compose chips, kebab menus) inherit
   351	    // the contract without re-touching this handler.
   352	    row.addEventListener('keydown', (ev) => {
   353	      if (ev.key !== 'Enter' && ev.key !== ' ') return;
   354	      if (
   355	        ev.target instanceof Element
   356	        && ev.target.closest(
   357	          'button, a[href], input, select, textarea, [role="button"]:not([data-rail-lane])',
   358	        ) !== null
   359	      ) {
   360	        return;
   361	      }
   362	      ev.preventDefault();
   363	      handleRailRowActivation(state, projectKey, id);
   364	    });
   365	  }
   366	}
   367	
   368	function bindSwimStubs(state: SwimlaneState, projectKey: string): void {
   369	  for (const stub of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>(
   370	    '[data-swim-stub]',
   371	  )) {
   372	    const id = stub.dataset.swimStub;
   373	    if (id === undefined) continue;
   374	    stub.addEventListener('click', () => {
   375	      if (state.hidden.has(id)) return; // shouldn't be reachable; defensive
   376	      state.focused.add(id);
   377	      applyState(state);
   378	      persist(state, projectKey);
   379	    });
   380	  }
   381	}
   382	
   383	/**
   384	 * Build a fresh `SwimlaneState` from current localStorage + URL +
   385	 * live lane set. Factored out of `initSwimlane` so the preset
   386	 * controller (Task 5.5) can rebuild state from storage without
   387	 * re-binding click handlers — the preset apply pipeline writes
   388	 * through the constituent storage keys and then calls
   389	 * `reapplyFromStorage` to push DOM into the new state. The bound
   390	 * handlers' closure-captured state object is mutated in-place so

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	/**
     2	 * Per-lane Compose chip + empty-lane CTA controller (Phase 5
     3	 * Task 5.1C + Task 5.2).
     4	 *
     5	 * Wires TWO clipboard-only affordances inside every swim:
     6	 *
     7	 *   - `.swim-compose` chip in the swim-head (Task 5.1C). Composes
     8	 *     `/deskwork:add <SLUG> --lane <laneId> --stage <firstStage>`
     9	 *     — the literal four-character `<SLUG>` placeholder is part of
    10	 *     the copied text, the operator replaces it in the chat editor
    11	 *     after paste.
    12	 *   - `.swim-empty-cta .sec-cta` button in the empty-lane body
    13	 *     (Task 5.2). Composes `/deskwork:add --lane <laneId>` — NO
    14	 *     slug placeholder, NO `--stage` flag (the operator's first
    15	 *     invocation in a lane runs the add skill's full prompt flow).
    16	 *
    17	 * Both affordances:
    18	 *
    19	 *   - Use `navigator.clipboard.writeText` as the entire side effect.
    20	 *     On success they flash `.copied` (visual + aria-label swap)
    21	 *     for ~2000ms, then revert.
    22	 *   - Stop click propagation so the parent `.swim-head` / swim body
    23	 *     handlers don't also fire (the lane-collapse toggler would
    24	 *     otherwise pick the click up).
    25	 *   - Honor collapse precedence: when the parent swim is `.collapsed`,
    26	 *     click is a no-op.
    27	 *   - Activate on Space (with `preventDefault` to suppress page
    28	 *     scroll) per WCAG 2.1 SC 2.1.1. Enter is free via the native
    29	 *     `<button>` keyboard contract.
    30	 *
    31	 * Per THESIS Consequence 2 + DESKWORK-STATE-MACHINE.md Commandment
    32	 * II: the studio does NOT mutate sidecar state from either
    33	 * affordance. No verb is dispatched, no network request is made, no
    34	 * entry is created. The operator's pasted slash command IS the
    35	 * action — this controller's contract is clipboard + flash, period.
    36	 *
    37	 * Per the no-fallback rule: when `navigator.clipboard` is missing
    38	 * or `writeText` rejects, the controller surfaces a runtime error
    39	 * rather than papering over with `document.execCommand('copy')`.
    40	 * The error is the correct signal that the surface is broken.
    41	 */
    42	
    43	/** Duration the affordance stays in the `.copied` flash state (ms). */
    44	const COPIED_FLASH_MS = 2000;
    45	
    46	/** Literal slug placeholder — operator replaces it in the chat editor. */
    47	const SLUG_PLACEHOLDER = '<SLUG>';
    48	
    49	/** Accessible name for an affordance during the `.copied` flash. */
    50	const COPIED_ARIA_LABEL = 'Copied — paste in chat';
    51	
    52	/** WeakMap of button → pending revert-timer handle. */
    53	const pendingTimers = new WeakMap<HTMLButtonElement, number>();
    54	
    55	/**
    56	 * Snapshot of an affordance's render-time `aria-label` so the
    57	 * `.copied` flash can swap it to the success message and restore it
    58	 * on revert. Captured at bind time so subsequent renders / DOM
    59	 * rewrites don't drift the snapshot.
    60	 *
    61	 * Mobile motivation: on phone the compose chip's `.sc-label` is
    62	 * `display: none`, so the visible label swap is invisible to
    63	 * screen-reader users — `aria-label` is the only accessible name.
    64	 * Without this swap the AT user gets zero feedback that the copy
    65	 * succeeded. The empty-CTA's `.sec-label` is visible at every
    66	 * breakpoint, but mirroring the swap keeps the contract uniform.
    67	 */
    68	const originalAriaLabel = new WeakMap<HTMLButtonElement, string>();
    69	
    70	/**
    71	 * Per-affordance behavior contract. Each affordance kind (compose
    72	 * chip vs empty CTA) provides its own slash-command builder + flash
    73	 * visual swap (the chip is "+ new" → "✓ Copied — paste in chat";
    74	 * the CTA is "Create your first entry" → "Copied — paste in chat").
    75	 */
    76	interface AffordanceSpec {
    77	  /** CSS selector the controller targets to bind this affordance. */
    78	  readonly selector: string;
    79	  /**
    80	   * Compose the slash command to copy. Receives the affordance's
    81	   * dataset; returns the literal text written to the clipboard.
    82	   */
    83	  readonly compose: (dataset: DOMStringMap) => string;
    84	  /** Apply the `.copied` visual swap (icon + label). */
    85	  readonly enterCopied: (button: HTMLButtonElement) => void;
    86	  /** Restore the at-rest visual state (icon + label). */
    87	  readonly leaveCopied: (button: HTMLButtonElement) => void;
    88	}
    89	
    90	function composeChipSlash(dataset: DOMStringMap): string {
    91	  const { laneId, firstStage } = dataset;
    92	  if (laneId === undefined || firstStage === undefined) {
    93	    throw new Error(
    94	      '.swim-compose chip missing data-lane-id or data-first-stage',
    95	    );
    96	  }
    97	  return `/deskwork:add ${SLUG_PLACEHOLDER} --lane ${laneId} --stage ${firstStage}`;
    98	}
    99	
   100	function composeEmptyCtaSlash(dataset: DOMStringMap): string {
   101	  const { laneId } = dataset;
   102	  if (laneId === undefined) {
   103	    throw new Error('.swim-empty-cta .sec-cta missing data-lane-id');
   104	  }
   105	  return `/deskwork:add --lane ${laneId}`;
   106	}
   107	
   108	function chipEnterCopied(button: HTMLButtonElement): void {
   109	  const icon = button.querySelector<HTMLElement>('.sc-icon');
   110	  const label = button.querySelector<HTMLElement>('.sc-label');
   111	  if (icon !== null) icon.textContent = '✓';
   112	  if (label !== null) label.textContent = 'Copied — paste in chat';
   113	}
   114	
   115	function chipLeaveCopied(button: HTMLButtonElement): void {
   116	  const icon = button.querySelector<HTMLElement>('.sc-icon');
   117	  const label = button.querySelector<HTMLElement>('.sc-label');
   118	  if (icon !== null) icon.textContent = '+';
   119	  if (label !== null) label.textContent = 'new';
   120	}
   121	
   122	function ctaEnterCopied(button: HTMLButtonElement): void {
   123	  const icon = button.querySelector<HTMLElement>('.sec-icon');
   124	  const label = button.querySelector<HTMLElement>('.sec-label');
   125	  if (icon !== null) icon.textContent = '✓';
   126	  if (label !== null) label.textContent = 'Copied — paste in chat';
   127	}
   128	
   129	function ctaLeaveCopied(button: HTMLButtonElement): void {
   130	  const icon = button.querySelector<HTMLElement>('.sec-icon');
   131	  const label = button.querySelector<HTMLElement>('.sec-label');
   132	  if (icon !== null) icon.textContent = '+';
   133	  if (label !== null) label.textContent = 'Create your first entry';
   134	}
   135	
   136	const COMPOSE_CHIP_SPEC: AffordanceSpec = {
   137	  selector: '.swim-compose[data-swim-compose]',
   138	  compose: composeChipSlash,
   139	  enterCopied: chipEnterCopied,
   140	  leaveCopied: chipLeaveCopied,
   141	};
   142	
   143	const EMPTY_CTA_SPEC: AffordanceSpec = {
   144	  selector: '.swim-empty-cta .sec-cta[data-swim-empty-copy]',
   145	  compose: composeEmptyCtaSlash,
   146	  enterCopied: ctaEnterCopied,
   147	  leaveCopied: ctaLeaveCopied,
   148	};
   149	
   150	function enterCopiedState(button: HTMLButtonElement, spec: AffordanceSpec): void {
   151	  button.classList.add('copied');
   152	  button.setAttribute('aria-label', COPIED_ARIA_LABEL);
   153	  spec.enterCopied(button);
   154	}
   155	
   156	function leaveCopiedState(button: HTMLButtonElement, spec: AffordanceSpec): void {
   157	  button.classList.remove('copied');
   158	  const original = originalAriaLabel.get(button);
   159	  if (original !== undefined) button.setAttribute('aria-label', original);
   160	  spec.leaveCopied(button);
   161	}
   162	
   163	/**
   164	 * Schedule the revert. Any prior revert-timer on this button is
   165	 * cleared first so rapid double-clicks restart the flash window —
   166	 * the affordance stays in `.copied` for ~2000ms after the LAST
   167	 * click, not after the first.
   168	 */
   169	function scheduleRevert(button: HTMLButtonElement, spec: AffordanceSpec): void {
   170	  const prior = pendingTimers.get(button);
   171	  if (prior !== undefined) window.clearTimeout(prior);
   172	  const handle = window.setTimeout(() => {
   173	    pendingTimers.delete(button);
   174	    leaveCopiedState(button, spec);
   175	  }, COPIED_FLASH_MS);
   176	  pendingTimers.set(button, handle);
   177	}
   178	
   179	/**
   180	 * Perform the clipboard write + transition into the flash state.
   181	 *
   182	 * Per the no-fallback rule: if `navigator.clipboard` is unavailable
   183	 * OR `writeText` rejects, the error propagates. We do not swallow
   184	 * the failure with `document.execCommand('copy')` or any other
   185	 * degraded path — the operator seeing the surface as broken is the
   186	 * correct signal.
   187	 */
   188	async function copyAndFlash(
   189	  button: HTMLButtonElement,
   190	  spec: AffordanceSpec,
   191	): Promise<void> {
   192	  // `navigator.clipboard` is missing on http (non-secure) contexts
   193	  // and in jsdom without an explicit shim. Surface the missing API
   194	  // as a runtime error per the no-fallback rule.
   195	  if (typeof navigator.clipboard?.writeText !== 'function') {
   196	    throw new Error(
   197	      'navigator.clipboard.writeText is unavailable — the .swim-'
   198	      + 'compose chip requires a secure (https) context',
   199	    );
   200	  }
   201	  const text = spec.compose(button.dataset);
   202	  await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
   203	  enterCopiedState(button, spec);
   204	  scheduleRevert(button, spec);
   205	}
   206	
   207	/**
   208	 * Resolve an affordance-activation gesture (click OR Space keydown).
   209	 * Returns false when collapse precedence blocks the gesture; throws
   210	 * the underlying clipboard error otherwise so the caller (and any
   211	 * test that spies on rejection) sees the failure.
   212	 */
   213	async function activateAffordance(
   214	  button: HTMLButtonElement,
   215	  spec: AffordanceSpec,
   216	): Promise<boolean> {
   217	  const swim = button.closest<HTMLElement>('.swim[data-lane-id]');
   218	  if (swim !== null && swim.classList.contains('collapsed')) return false;
   219	  await copyAndFlash(button, spec);
   220	  return true;

    40	 * — exactly one cell is `aria-checked="true"` per group.

    42	
    43	import {
    44	  readStoredObjectMap,
    45	  resolveProjectKey,
    46	  STORAGE_KEY_PREFIX,
    47	} from './swimlane-storage.ts';
    48	
    49	const VIEW_MODE_KEY_SUFFIX = ':view-mode';
    50	
    51	/**
    52	 * Mobile breakpoint shared with the layout side. Mobile-list /
    53	 * desktop-kanban defaults are the spec contract (see the brief at
    54	 * `docs/studio-design/ACCEPTED/2026-05-27-multi-lane-dashboard-d3
    55	 * -press-bay/brief.md` § "Implementation notes"). The 720px value
    56	 * matches the `@media (max-width: 720px)` rule in
    57	 * `dashboard-swimlane-mobile.css` so the view-default flips at
    58	 * exactly the viewport size the layout collapses.
    59	 */
    60	const MOBILE_MEDIA_QUERY = '(max-width: 720px)';
    61	
    62	type ViewMode = 'kanban' | 'list';
    63	
    64	function isViewMode(value: unknown): value is ViewMode {
    65	  return value === 'kanban' || value === 'list';
    66	}
    67	
    68	function viewModeKey(projectKey: string): string {
    69	  return STORAGE_KEY_PREFIX + projectKey + VIEW_MODE_KEY_SUFFIX;
    70	}
    71	
    72	function readStoredOverrides(key: string): Map<string, ViewMode> {
    73	  return readStoredObjectMap(key, isViewMode);
    74	}
    75	
    76	function writeStoredOverrides(
    77	  key: string,
    78	  overrides: ReadonlyMap<string, ViewMode>,
    79	): void {
    80	  try {
    81	    const obj: Record<string, ViewMode> = {};
    82	    for (const [laneId, mode] of overrides) {
    83	      obj[laneId] = mode;
    84	    }
    85	    window.localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(obj));
    86	  } catch {
    87	    // localStorage unavailable — in-page state still works.
    88	  }
    89	}
    90	
    91	/**
    92	 * Resolve the effective view-mode for a lane: per-lane override
    93	 * wins if present; otherwise the viewport-aware default applies
    94	 * (mobile→list, desktop→kanban).
    95	 */
    96	function resolveMode(
    97	  laneId: string,
    98	  overrides: ReadonlyMap<string, ViewMode>,
    99	  isMobile: boolean,
   100	): ViewMode {
   101	  const override = overrides.get(laneId);
   102	  if (override !== undefined) return override;
   103	  return isMobile ? 'list' : 'kanban';
   104	}
   105	
   106	/**
   107	 * Apply the effective view-mode for one swim: swap `.view-kanban`
   108	 * / `.view-list` classes on the swim, and mirror `aria-checked`
   109	 * across the two `.vt-cell` cells in its toggle.
   110	 */
   111	function applySwimMode(swim: HTMLElement, mode: ViewMode): void {
   112	  swim.classList.toggle('view-kanban', mode === 'kanban');
   113	  swim.classList.toggle('view-list', mode === 'list');
   114	  const cells = swim.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>(
   115	    '.view-toggle .vt-cell[data-view-mode]',
   116	  );
   117	  for (const cell of cells) {
   118	    const cellMode = cell.dataset.viewMode;
   119	    const checked = cellMode === mode;
   120	    cell.setAttribute('aria-checked', checked ? 'true' : 'false');
   121	    cell.classList.toggle('active', checked);
   122	  }
   123	}
   124	
   125	/**
   126	 * Apply collapse-precedence to every swim: when a swim has
   127	 * `.collapsed`, stamp `aria-disabled="true"` on each toggle cell.
   128	 * The class on the swim is owned by `swimlane-collapse.ts`; this
   129	 * controller observes it (via a MutationObserver) so the aria
   130	 * state stays in lockstep.
   131	 */
   132	function applyCollapseFlag(swim: HTMLElement): void {
   133	  const collapsed = swim.classList.contains('collapsed');
   134	  const cells = swim.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>(
   135	    '.view-toggle .vt-cell[data-view-mode]',
   136	  );
   137	  for (const cell of cells) {
   138	    cell.setAttribute('aria-disabled', collapsed ? 'true' : 'false');
   139	  }
   140	}
   141	
   142	function applyAll(
   143	  overrides: ReadonlyMap<string, ViewMode>,
   144	  isMobile: boolean,
   145	): void {
   146	  for (const swim of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>('.swim[data-lane-id]')) {
   147	    const laneId = swim.dataset.laneId;
   148	    if (laneId === undefined) continue;
   149	    const mode = resolveMode(laneId, overrides, isMobile);
   150	    applySwimMode(swim, mode);
   151	    applyCollapseFlag(swim);
   152	  }
   153	}
   154	
   155	interface ViewToggleState {
   156	  /** Per-lane operator overrides; per-lane override > viewport default. */
   157	  readonly overrides: Map<string, ViewMode>;
   158	  /** Current viewport-class (true when narrower than the breakpoint). */
   159	  isMobile: boolean;
   160	}
   161	
   162	/**
   163	 * Resolve a cell-activation gesture (click OR Space keydown) into
   164	 * a (laneId, mode) tuple, then write the override + reapply + persist.
   165	 * Returns false when the gesture is invalid (missing data attrs) or
   166	 * blocked by collapse precedence (parent swim has `.collapsed`).
   167	 *
   168	 * Factored out of the click + keydown handler bodies (which were
   169	 * identical save for the event-prep step) so the dispatch logic
   170	 * lives in one place.
   171	 */
   172	function activateCell(
   173	  cell: HTMLButtonElement,
   174	  state: ViewToggleState,
   175	  projectKey: string,
   176	): boolean {
   177	  const laneId = cell.dataset.laneId;
   178	  const mode = cell.dataset.viewMode;
   179	  if (laneId === undefined || !isViewMode(mode)) return false;
   180	  // Collapse precedence: when the parent swim is collapsed, the
   181	  // gesture is a no-op. The CSS rule disables pointer events too,
   182	  // but this guard makes the contract explicit + the jsdom test
   183	  // path doesn't honor CSS pointer-events.
   184	  const swim = cell.closest<HTMLElement>('.swim[data-lane-id]');
   185	  if (swim !== null && swim.classList.contains('collapsed')) return false;
   186	  state.overrides.set(laneId, mode);
   187	  applyAll(state.overrides, state.isMobile);
   188	  writeStoredOverrides(viewModeKey(projectKey), state.overrides);
   189	  return true;
   190	}
   191	
   192	function bindCellClicks(
   193	  state: ViewToggleState,
   194	  projectKey: string,
   195	): void {
   196	  for (const cell of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>(
   197	    '.view-toggle .vt-cell[data-view-mode]',
   198	  )) {
   199	    cell.addEventListener('click', (ev) => {
   200	      // Stop the click from bubbling into `swimlane-collapse.ts`'s
   201	      // swim-head handler, which would otherwise also toggle the
   202	      // lane collapse on every cell click (the cells live inside
   203	      // the swim-head DOM tree).
   204	      ev.stopPropagation();
   205	      activateCell(cell, state, projectKey);
   206	    });
   207	    cell.addEventListener('keydown', (ev) => {
   208	      if (ev.key !== ' ') return;
   209	      // Space activates the radio cell. Per WCAG 2.1 SC 2.1.1,
   210	      // preventDefault to suppress page scroll. Enter is free
   211	      // with the native `<button>` keyboard contract — no extra
   212	      // handler needed.
   213	      ev.preventDefault();
   214	      activateCell(cell, state, projectKey);
   215	    });
   216	  }
   217	}
   218	
   219	/**
   220	 * Observe each swim's class list so the toggle's `aria-disabled`
   221	 * flips when `swimlane-collapse.ts` adds/removes `.collapsed`.
   222	 * The class is owned externally; the observer keeps the toggle's
   223	 * a11y state in lockstep without re-binding click handlers.
   224	 */
   225	function observeCollapseClassChanges(): void {
   226	  if (typeof MutationObserver === 'undefined') return;
   227	  const obs = new MutationObserver((records) => {
   228	    for (const r of records) {
   229	      const target = r.target;
   230	      if (!(target instanceof HTMLElement)) continue;
   231	      if (!target.classList.contains('swim')) continue;
   232	      applyCollapseFlag(target);
   233	    }
   234	  });
   235	  for (const swim of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>('.swim[data-lane-id]')) {
   236	    obs.observe(swim, { attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['class'] });
   237	  }
   238	}
   239	
   240	function watchViewport(state: ViewToggleState): void {
   241	  if (typeof window.matchMedia !== 'function') return;
   242	  const mql = window.matchMedia(MOBILE_MEDIA_QUERY);
   243	  // matchMedia.addEventListener is the modern API; older browsers
   244	  // exposed `addListener`. We only call the modern API — if it's
   245	  // unavailable, the viewport-default applies on initial paint and
   246	  // doesn't re-flow on resize, which is acceptable (the operator
   247	  // can still flip the toggle by hand and the override persists).
   248	  if (typeof mql.addEventListener === 'function') {
   249	    mql.addEventListener('change', (ev) => {
   250	      state.isMobile = ev.matches;
   251	      applyAll(state.overrides, state.isMobile);
   252	    });
   253	  }
   254	}
   255	
   256	/**
   257	 * Module-level singleton — written by `initSwimlaneViewToggle`,
   258	 * mutated in-place by `reapplyViewToggleFromStorage` so the bound
   259	 * `.vt-cell` click handlers (which closure-capture the state object)
   260	 * keep operating on the same overrides Map after a preset apply.
   261	 *
   262	 * Per AUDIT-20260528-37 (F5): tests that mutate this singleton must
   263	 * reset DOM + storage in `beforeEach` so cross-describe-block state
   264	 * does not leak. Re-invoking `initSwimlaneViewToggle` after the
   265	 * reset reassigns the singleton — that is the sanctioned reset path.
   266	 */
   267	let activeState: ViewToggleState | null = null;
   268	
   269	/**
   270	 * Re-read storage + re-apply to every swim. Used by the Task 5.5
   271	 * preset controller after writing through the view-mode storage
   272	 * key. No-op when `initSwimlaneViewToggle` hasn't fired yet.
   273	 */
   274	export function reapplyViewToggleFromStorage(): void {
   275	  if (activeState === null) return;
   276	  const shell = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>('[data-bay-shell]');
   277	  if (shell === null) return;
   278	  const projectKey = resolveProjectKey(shell);
   279	  const next = readStoredOverrides(viewModeKey(projectKey));
   280	  // Mutate the singleton's overrides Map in-place so bound handlers
   281	  // observe the new entries through their closure-captured reference.
   282	  activeState.overrides.clear();
   283	  for (const [k, v] of next) activeState.overrides.set(k, v);
   284	  applyAll(activeState.overrides, activeState.isMobile);
   285	}
   286	
   287	/**
   288	 * Entry point — wire view-toggle handlers + restore the operator's
   289	 * resolved view-mode for every swim on the page. No-op when the
   290	 * bay-shell is absent.
   291	 */
   292	export function initSwimlaneViewToggle(): void {
   293	  const shell = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>('[data-bay-shell]');
   294	  if (shell === null) return;
   295	
   296	  const projectKey = resolveProjectKey(shell);
   297	  const overrides = readStoredOverrides(viewModeKey(projectKey));
   298	  const isMobile = typeof window.matchMedia === 'function'
   299	    ? window.matchMedia(MOBILE_MEDIA_QUERY).matches
   300	    : false;
   301	
   302	  const state: ViewToggleState = {
   303	    overrides,
   304	    isMobile,
   305	  };
   306	  activeState = state;
   307	
   308	  applyAll(state.overrides, state.isMobile);
   309	  bindCellClicks(state, projectKey);
   310	  observeCollapseClassChanges();
   311	  watchViewport(state);
   312	}

   271	/**
   272	 * Per-lane Compose chip (Task 5.1C). Renders the `+ new` affordance
   273	 * in the swim-head, between the view-toggle and the lane-collapse
   274	 * chevron. Clicking the chip clipboard-copies the partial slash
   275	 * command `/deskwork:add <SLUG> --lane <laneId> --stage <firstStage>`
   276	 * — the literal four-character `<SLUG>` placeholder is part of the
   277	 * copied text, the operator replaces it in the chat editor after
   278	 * paste.
   279	 *
   280	 * Per THESIS Consequence 2 and DESKWORK-STATE-MACHINE.md Commandment
   281	 * II — the chip is a clipboard convenience, never a verb. No sidecar
   282	 * mutation, no network round trip, no state change. The operator's
   283	 * pasted slash command IS the action.
   284	 *
   285	 * Per `affordance-placement.md` — the chip lives ON the lane it
   286	 * composes for, not in any toolbar.
   287	 *
   288	 * `firstLinearStage` is the entry's destination stage on `/deskwork
   289	 * :add`. The pipeline-template schema enforces `linearStages.length
   290	 * ≥ 1` (`packages/core/src/pipelines/types.ts:99` —
   291	 * `uniqueStringArray('linearStages', 1)`), so every lane has at
   292	 * least one. The render throws if that invariant is ever violated
   293	 * at runtime — per the no-fallback rule, surfacing the empty case
   294	 * as an error rather than silently emitting an empty `data-first-
   295	 * stage` attribute.
   296	 */
   297	export function renderComposeChip(
   298	  laneId: string,
   299	  laneName: string,
   300	  firstLinearStage: string,
   301	): RawHtml {
   302	  return unsafe(html`
   303	    <button class="swim-compose" type="button"
   304	      aria-label="Compose new entry in ${laneName}"
   305	      data-swim-compose
   306	      data-lane-id="${laneId}"
   307	      data-first-stage="${firstLinearStage}">
   308	      <span class="sc-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
   309	      <span class="sc-label">new</span>
   310	    </button>`);
   311	}
   312	
   313	/**
   314	 * Per-lane empty-lane CTA (Task 5.2 Step 5.2.2). Rendered only
   315	 * when `bucket.entryCount === 0` — the prominent "create your
   316	 * first entry" affordance an operator sees the first time they
   317	 * open a freshly-configured lane.
   318	 *
   319	 * Sibling to the per-lane `.swim-compose` chip (Task 5.1C) but
   320	 * with a DIFFERENT clipboard payload:
   321	 *
   322	 *   - `.swim-compose` chip → `/deskwork:add <SLUG> --lane <id>
   323	 *     --stage <first-stage>` (the operator already knows what
   324	 *     they're composing; the chip carries an explicit destination
   325	 *     stage to skip).
   326	 *   - `.swim-empty-cta` button → `/deskwork:add --lane <id>` (no
   327	 *     `<SLUG>` placeholder, no `--stage` flag — the operator's
   328	 *     first invocation in this lane; the add skill prompts for
   329	 *     slug + content as part of its normal flow).
   330	 *
   331	 * Per THESIS Consequence 2 and DESKWORK-STATE-MACHINE.md Commandment
   332	 * II — clipboard only; no sidecar mutation, no network round trip.
   333	 *
   334	 * Per `affordance-placement.md` — the CTA lives ON the empty lane's
   335	 * swim body (between `.swim-head` and `.swim-compact`), not in any
   336	 * toolbar. Mirrors the `.er-outline-tab` precedent of attaching
   337	 * affordances ON the component they affect.
   338	 */
   339	export function renderEmptyLaneCta(
   340	  laneId: string,
   341	  laneName: string,
   342	): RawHtml {
   343	  return unsafe(html`
   344	    <div class="swim-empty-cta" data-swim-empty-cta>
   345	      <p class="sec-msg">Create your first entry in this lane.</p>
   346	      <button class="sec-cta" type="button"
   347	        aria-label="Compose first entry in ${laneName}"
   348	        data-swim-empty-copy
   349	        data-lane-id="${laneId}">
   350	        <span class="sec-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
   351	        <span class="sec-label">Create your first entry</span>
   352	      </button>
   353	      <p class="sec-hint">copies <code>/deskwork:add --lane ${laneId}</code> to your clipboard</p>
   354	    </div>`);
   355	}
   356	
   357	function renderSwimCompact(bucket: LaneBucket): RawHtml {
   358	  const stages: string[] = [
   359	    ...bucket.template.linearStages,
   360	    ...bucket.template.offPipelineStages,
   361	  ];
   362	  // `lockedStages` is optional on a pipeline template (schema:
   363	  // `uniqueStringArray('lockedStages', 0).optional()`). Treat
   364	  // missing as "no stages locked" — an empty lookup set, never
   365	  // an "every stage locked" sentinel.
   366	  const lockedSet = new Set<string>(bucket.template.lockedStages ?? []);
   367	  const cellsRaw = stages
   368	    .map((stage) => {
   369	      const count = (bucket.byStage.get(stage) ?? []).length;
   370	      const empty = count === 0 ? ' empty' : '';
   371	      const locked = lockedSet.has(stage) ? ' locked' : '';
   372	      return html`
   373	        <div class="sc-stage${unsafe(empty)}${unsafe(locked)}" data-sc-stage="${stage}">
   374	          <span class="sc-name">${stage}</span>
   375	          <span class="sc-count">${count}</span>
   376	        </div>`;
   377	    })
   378	    .join('');
   379	  return unsafe(html`
   380	    <div class="swim-compact" data-swim-compact>${unsafe(cellsRaw)}</div>`);

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/dashboard/swimlane-storage.ts | sed -n '1,120p'" in /Users/orion/work/deskwork-work/graphical-entries
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	/**
     2	 * Shared localStorage helpers for the dashboard swimlane controllers.
     3	 *
     4	 * The `swimlane.ts`, `swimlane-collapse.ts`, and `swimlane-view-
     5	 * toggle.ts` controllers all namespace localStorage entries under
     6	 * `deskwork:dashboard:<projectKey>:<suffix>` and all resolve the
     7	 * `<projectKey>` from the bay-shell's `data-project-key` attribute
     8	 * (falling back to the page pathname when the shell lacks one). The
     9	 * map-shaped controllers (collapse + view-toggle) additionally read
    10	 * a `Map<laneId, T>` whose on-disk shape is a JSON object. This
    11	 * module centralises all three pieces — the key prefix, the project-
    12	 * key resolver, and the read+parse boilerplate — so the controllers
    13	 * import a single contract instead of redeclaring it.
    14	 *
    15	 * Failures (no entry / malformed JSON / wrong root type / unknown
    16	 * value shape) all collapse to "empty map" — the controllers treat
    17	 * localStorage as best-effort persistence; in-page state still
    18	 * works without it.
    19	 */
    20	
    21	/**
    22	 * Common prefix for every dashboard localStorage key. Controllers
    23	 * append `:<projectKey>:<suffix>` to namespace per-operator state
    24	 * per-project (so two operators sharing a machine but working on
    25	 * different projects don't see each other's lane state).
    26	 */
    27	export const STORAGE_KEY_PREFIX = 'deskwork:dashboard:';
    28	
    29	/**
    30	 * Resolve the project key the swimlane controllers use to namespace
    31	 * localStorage entries. The bay-shell carries it as `data-project-
    32	 * key`; in jsdom + tests with no shell, fall back to the page
    33	 * pathname for stable isolation.
    34	 */
    35	export function resolveProjectKey(shell: HTMLElement): string {
    36	  const explicit = shell.dataset.projectKey;
    37	  if (explicit !== undefined && explicit.length > 0) return explicit;
    38	  return window.location.pathname;
    39	}
    40	
    41	/**
    42	 * Read a JSON array of strings from localStorage. Returns null on
    43	 * any read failure (missing entry, parse error, wrong root shape).
    44	 * Non-string array elements are dropped. Callers pick their own
    45	 * container type — `swimlane.ts:readStoredSet` projects into a
    46	 * `Set<string>`; `swimlane-drag.ts:readStoredOrder` keeps the
    47	 * positional array (lane order is positional, not set-like).
    48	 *
    49	 * Centralising the read+parse boilerplate avoids drift between the
    50	 * two surfaces while letting each caller pick the in-memory shape
    51	 * that matches its access pattern.
    52	 */
    53	export function readStoredStringArray(key: string): readonly string[] | null {
    54	  try {
    55	    const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(key);
    56	    if (raw === null) return null;
    57	    const parsed: unknown = JSON.parse(raw);
    58	    if (!Array.isArray(parsed)) return null;
    59	    const out: string[] = [];
    60	    for (const item of parsed) {
    61	      if (typeof item === 'string') out.push(item);
    62	    }
    63	    return out;
    64	  } catch {
    65	    return null;
    66	  }
    67	}
    68	
    69	/**
    70	 * Read a JSON object from localStorage and project it into a
    71	 * `Map<string, T>` via a per-value type guard. Returns an empty
    72	 * Map on every read failure (missing entry, parse error, wrong
    73	 * root shape).
    74	 *
    75	 * The value-side guard lets each caller declare its own allowed
    76	 * value shape (e.g. `(v): v is ViewMode => v === 'kanban' || v ===
    77	 * 'list'`) without leaking the typed result through a cast.
    78	 */
    79	export function readStoredObjectMap<T>(
    80	  key: string,
    81	  isValidValue: (value: unknown) => value is T,
    82	): Map<string, T> {
    83	  try {
    84	    const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(key);
    85	    if (raw === null) return new Map();
    86	    const parsed: unknown = JSON.parse(raw);
    87	    if (parsed === null || typeof parsed !== 'object' || Array.isArray(parsed)) {
    88	      return new Map();
    89	    }
    90	    const out = new Map<string, T>();
    91	    for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(parsed)) {
    92	      if (isValidValue(v)) out.set(k, v);
    93	    }
    94	    return out;
    95	  } catch {
    96	    return new Map();
    97	  }
    98	}

   382	
   383	/**
   384	 * Build a fresh `SwimlaneState` from current localStorage + URL +
   385	 * live lane set. Factored out of `initSwimlane` so the preset
   386	 * controller (Task 5.5) can rebuild state from storage without
   387	 * re-binding click handlers — the preset apply pipeline writes
   388	 * through the constituent storage keys and then calls
   389	 * `reapplyFromStorage` to push DOM into the new state. The bound
   390	 * handlers' closure-captured state object is mutated in-place so
   391	 * subsequent click/keyboard gestures see the same focused + hidden
   392	 * sets the DOM reflects.
   393	 */
   394	function buildStateFromStorage(
   395	  allLanes: readonly string[],
   396	  projectKey: string,
   397	  honorUrlFocus: boolean,
   398	): SwimlaneState {
   399	  const urlFocus = honorUrlFocus ? parseFocusFromUrl() : null;
   400	  const storedFocus = readStoredSet(focusKey(projectKey));
   401	  const storedHidden = readStoredSet(visibilityKey(projectKey)) ?? new Set<string>();
   402	
   403	  let focused: Set<string>;
   404	  if (urlFocus !== null) {
   405	    focused = new Set<string>();
   406	    for (const id of urlFocus) {
   407	      if (allLanes.includes(id)) focused.add(id);
   408	    }
   409	  } else if (storedFocus !== null) {
   410	    focused = new Set<string>();
   411	    for (const id of storedFocus) {
   412	      if (allLanes.includes(id)) focused.add(id);
   413	    }
   414	  } else {
   415	    focused = new Set<string>(allLanes.filter((id) => !storedHidden.has(id)));
   416	  }
   417	
   418	  return {
   419	    focused,
   420	    hidden: storedHidden,
   421	    allLanes,
   422	  };
   423	}
   424	
   425	/**
   426	 * Module-level singleton state — written by `initSwimlane` and
   427	 * mutated by `reapplyFromStorage` so all bound handlers operate on
   428	 * the same object. Without the singleton, calling `reapplyFromStorage`
   429	 * would create a fresh state object that the already-bound click
   430	 * handlers wouldn't see — they'd keep mutating the original closure-
   431	 * captured object. The shared object pattern is the legitimate
   432	 * generalization the dispatch contract authorizes for Task 5.5's
   433	 * preset-application sequencing.
   434	 *
   435	 * Per AUDIT-20260528-37 (F5): tests that mutate this singleton must
   436	 * reset DOM + storage in `beforeEach` so cross-describe-block state
   437	 * does not leak. Re-invoking `initSwimlane` after the reset
   438	 * reassigns the singleton — that is the sanctioned reset path.
   439	 */
   440	let activeState: SwimlaneState | null = null;
   441	
   442	/**
   443	 * Re-read storage and re-apply the resulting state to the DOM. Used
   444	 * by the Task 5.5 preset controller after writing through the
   445	 * visibility + focus storage keys. URL `?focus=` is NOT honored on
   446	 * re-apply — preset application is the authoritative source on this
   447	 * call (the URL was honored once at initial paint).
   448	 */
   449	export function reapplyFromStorage(): void {
   450	  if (activeState === null) return;
   451	  const shell = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>('[data-bay-shell]');
   452	  if (shell === null) return;
   453	  const projectKey = resolveProjectKey(shell);
   454	  const next = buildStateFromStorage(activeState.allLanes, projectKey, false);
   455	  // Mutate the singleton in-place so already-bound click handlers
   456	  // observe the new sets through their closure-captured reference.
   457	  activeState.focused.clear();
   458	  for (const id of next.focused) activeState.focused.add(id);
   459	  activeState.hidden.clear();
   460	  for (const id of next.hidden) activeState.hidden.add(id);
   461	  applyState(activeState);
   462	}

   468	 */
   469	export function initSwimlane(): void {
   470	  const shell = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>('[data-bay-shell]');

 succeeded in 0ms:

   223	/**
   224	 * Surface a clipboard / activation error as a synchronously-thrown
   225	 * error in the next microtask, so it lands on `window.onerror`
   226	 * rather than escaping as an unhandled rejection. The no-fallback
   227	 * contract requires the failure be visible — `window.onerror` is
   228	 * the strongest visible surface a click handler can produce without
   229	 * blocking the event loop. The error type is preserved.
   230	 */
   231	function surfaceActivationError(err: unknown): void {
   232	  queueMicrotask(() => {
   233	    if (err instanceof Error) throw err;
   234	    throw new Error(String(err));
   235	  });
   236	}
   237	
   238	function bindAffordance(button: HTMLButtonElement, spec: AffordanceSpec): void {
   239	  const renderedAriaLabel = button.getAttribute('aria-label');
   240	  if (renderedAriaLabel !== null) {
   241	    originalAriaLabel.set(button, renderedAriaLabel);
   242	  }
   243	  button.addEventListener('click', (ev) => {
   244	    // Stop the click from bubbling into the swim-head /
   245	    // swim-body's collapse handler (which would otherwise also
   246	    // toggle the lane collapse on every affordance click).
   247	    ev.stopPropagation();
   248	    activateAffordance(button, spec).catch(surfaceActivationError);
   249	  });
   250	  button.addEventListener('keydown', (ev) => {
   251	    if (ev.key !== ' ') return;
   252	    // Suppress held-Space auto-repeat so a long press doesn't fire N
   253	    // clipboard writes (each keydown auto-repeat would otherwise re-
   254	    // invoke `activateAffordance`). The single-activation contract
   255	    // matches the click handler's one-shot semantics.
   256	    if (ev.repeat) return;
   257	    // Space activates the affordance. Per WCAG 2.1 SC 2.1.1,
   258	    // preventDefault to suppress page scroll. Enter is free with
   259	    // the native `<button>` keyboard contract — no extra handler
   260	    // needed.
   261	    ev.preventDefault();
   262	    activateAffordance(button, spec).catch(surfaceActivationError);
   263	  });
   264	}
   265	
   266	/**
   267	 * Entry point — wire compose-chip + empty-lane CTA handlers for
   268	 * every swim on the page. No-op when the bay-shell is absent.
   269	 */
   270	export function initSwimlaneCompose(): void {
   271	  const shell = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>('[data-bay-shell]');
   272	  if (shell === null) return;
   273	  for (const button of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>(
   274	    COMPOSE_CHIP_SPEC.selector,
   275	  )) {
   276	    bindAffordance(button, COMPOSE_CHIP_SPEC);
   277	  }
   278	  for (const button of document.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>(
   279	    EMPTY_CTA_SPEC.selector,
   280	  )) {
   281	    bindAffordance(button, EMPTY_CTA_SPEC);
   282	  }
   283	}

codex
### Compose chip copies an invalid command for stage names with spaces

Finding-ID: AUDIT-BARRAGE-codex-01
Status:     open
Severity:   medium
Surface:    plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/dashboard/swimlane-compose.ts:90-98; packages/studio/src/pages/dashboard/swimlane-card.ts:297-307

The copied command is assembled as `/deskwork:add <SLUG> --lane ${laneId} --stage ${firstStage}` with no argument quoting or escaping. That works for the current preset first stages (`Ideas`, `Sketched`, `Drafted`, etc.), but pipeline templates allow arbitrary non-empty stage strings, including names with spaces. A custom lane whose first stage is `QA Review` would copy `/deskwork:add <SLUG> --lane qa --stage QA Review`, which a normal argv parser reads as stage `QA` plus an extra `Review` token.

The server puts the raw first stage in `data-first-stage` at `swimlane-card.ts:303-307`, and the client serializes that value directly at `swimlane-compose.ts:90-98`. Fix by using the same command-argument quoting convention the slash-command parser expects, and add a regression with a custom template whose first linear stage contains whitespace and shell-sensitive characters.

### Dashboard localStorage has no schema/version segment despite version-bump reset being in scope

Finding-ID: AUDIT-BARRAGE-codex-02
Status:     open
Severity:   medium
Surface:    plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/dashboard/swimlane-storage.ts:21-27; plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/dashboard/swimlane.ts:64-69; plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/dashboard/swimlane-collapse.ts:60-65; plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/dashboard/swimlane-view-toggle.ts:68-70

The audit scope explicitly calls out “clear-on-version-bump,” but all persisted dashboard keys are stable forever under `deskwork:dashboard:<projectKey>:<suffix>`. The readers tolerate malformed JSON, but they do not distinguish old valid shapes from current valid shapes. If the meaning of `:focus`, `:visibility`, `:lane-collapse`, `:stage-collapse`, or `:view-mode` changes, old operator state continues to apply silently.

This is most visible in `STORAGE_KEY_PREFIX = 'deskwork:dashboard:'`; every controller appends only project key and suffix. A reasonable fix is to add a storage schema version to the prefix or store a version sentinel and clear the known swimlane keys when it mismatches. Tests should seed an older-version key and assert the controller ignores or removes it while preserving current-version state.

### Re-running swimlane initializers stacks duplicate event listeners with stale state closures

Finding-ID: AUDIT-BARRAGE-codex-03
Status:     open
Severity:   low
Surface:    plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/editorial-studio-client.ts:527-530; plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/dashboard/swimlane.ts:469-490; plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/dashboard/swimlane-collapse.ts:464-477; plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/dashboard/swimlane-view-toggle.ts:292-312; plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/dashboard/swimlane-compose.ts:270-282

`init()` calls four swimlane controllers, and each controller unconditionally binds listeners to existing DOM nodes. `initSwimlane` also replaces `activeState` at lines 480-481, while previously bound handlers still close over their older `state` object. The same shape exists in collapse, view-toggle, and compose: re-invocation binds again without a module guard or per-element sentinel.

Current page boot may call these once, but the code already introduces `reapply*FromStorage` paths and singleton state for client-side refresh-style operations. If a partial DOM re-init calls any initializer twice, clicks can fire multiple handlers and mutate different closure-captured state objects. Fix with per-controller idempotence: a module-level wired guard for whole-page singletons, or `dataset` sentinels per bound element when dynamic DOM replacement is expected.
